  <h1><a name="Analytics / Analytique">Analytics / Analytique</a></h1>
  <div class="method"><a name="putAnalytics"></a>
    <div class="method-path">
    <a class="up" href="#__Methods">Up</a>
    <pre class="post"><code class="huge"><span class="http-method">post</span> /analytics</code></pre></div>
    <div class="method-summary">Post analytics event to system / Enregistrer l'√©v√©nement analytique dans le syst√®me (<span class="nickname">putAnalytics</span>)</div>
    <div class="method-notes">Adds an Analytical event to the system / Ajoute un √©v√©nement analytique au syst√®me      Requires API Key / N√©cessite une cl√© API</div>


    <h3 class="field-label">Consumes</h3>
    This API call consumes the following media types via the <span class="header">Content-Type</span> request header:
    <ul>
      <li><code>application/json</code></li>
    </ul>

    <h3 class="field-label">Request body</h3>
    <div class="field-items">
      <div class="param">body <a href="#putanalytics_inner">putanalytics_inner</a> (optional)</div>

                </div>  <!-- field-items -->

    <h3 class="field-label">Request headers</h3>

    <h3 class="field-label">Query parameters</h3>
    <div class="field-items">
      <div class="param">search (optional)</div>
      
            <div class="param-desc"><span class="param-type">Query Parameter</span> &mdash; Record search term used / Enregistrement du terme de recherche utilis√© </div>      <div class="param">theme (optional)</div>
      
            <div class="param-desc"><span class="param-type">Query Parameter</span> &mdash; Record theme filter used / Enregistrer le filtre th√©matique utilis√© </div>      <div class="param">filter (optional)</div>
      
            <div class="param-desc"><span class="param-type">Query Parameter</span> &mdash; Record type filter used / Filtre de type d&#x27;enregistrement utilis√© </div>      <div class="param">geo (optional)</div>
      
            <div class="param-desc"><span class="param-type">Query Parameter</span> &mdash; Record geospatial bounding box used for search / Enregistrer la zone de d√©limitation g√©ospatiale utilis√©e pour la recherche </div>      <div class="param">uuid (optional)</div>
      
            <div class="param-desc"><span class="param-type">Query Parameter</span> &mdash; Record the UUID of accessed resource data / Enregistrer l&#x27;UUID des donn√©es acc√©d√©es </div>      <div class="param">resource (optional)</div>
      
            <div class="param-desc"><span class="param-type">Query Parameter</span> &mdash; Record the resouce of accessed data / Enregistrer la ressource des donn√©es consult√©es </div>      <div class="param">resource_type (optional)</div>
      
            <div class="param-desc"><span class="param-type">Query Parameter</span> &mdash; Record the resource type of accessed data / Enregistrer le type de ressource des donn√©es consult√©es </div>      <div class="param">loc (optional)</div>
      
            <div class="param-desc"><span class="param-type">Query Parameter</span> &mdash; Record location of analytics event / Enregistrer l&#x27;emplacement de l&#x27;√©v√©nement analytique </div>      <div class="param">lang (optional)</div>
      
            <div class="param-desc"><span class="param-type">Query Parameter</span> &mdash; Record language of event / Enregistrer la langue de l&#x27;√©v√©nement </div>      <div class="param">type (optional)</div>
      
            <div class="param-desc"><span class="param-type">Query Parameter</span> &mdash; Record type of analytics / Enregistrer le type d&#x27;analyse </div>      <div class="param">org (optional)</div>
      
            <div class="param-desc"><span class="param-type">Query Parameter</span> &mdash; Record organisation of accessed data / Organisation de l&#x27;enregistrement des donn√©es consult√©es </div>      <div class="param">foundational (optional)</div>
      
            <div class="param-desc"><span class="param-type">Query Parameter</span> &mdash; Record if dataset is foundational / Enregistrer si l&#x27;ensemble de donn√©es est fondamental </div>      <div class="param">type_filter (optional)</div>
      
            <div class="param-desc"><span class="param-type">Query Parameter</span> &mdash; Record if type filter was used / Enregistrer si le filtre de type a √©t√© utilis√© </div>    </div>  <!-- field-items -->

    <h3 class="field-label">Produces</h3>
    This API call produces the following media types according to the <span class="header">Accept</span> request header;
    the media type will be conveyed by the <span class="header">Content-Type</span> response header.
    <ul>
      <li><code>application/json</code></li>
    </ul>

        <a href="#geonetwork">geonetwork</a>

    <h3 class="field-label">Produces</h3>

    <h3 class="field-label">Responses</h3>
    <h4 class="field-label">200</h4>
    The metadata associated with foundational datasets / Les m√©tadonn√©es associ√©es aux ensembles de donn√©es fondamentales

  <hr/>
  <div class="method"><a name="geo"></a>
    <div class="method-path">
    <a class="up" href="#__Methods">Up</a>
    <pre class="get"><code class="huge"><span class="http-method">get</span> /geo</code></pre></div>
    <div class="method-summary">Geospatial and Keyword Search / Recherche g√©ospatiale et par mots-cl√©s (<span class="nickname">geo</span>)</div>
    <div class="method-notes">The API will take the keyword parameter and query the metadata fields applicable for keyword search. If the geospatial search is selected, the results are then ran through a geospatial intersect query based on the bounding box created from the north, east, south, and west parameters. The results returned are all metadata records containing the keyword that intersect with the bounding box. The result is an array of JSON objects. The API is bilingual, and passing the parameter of lang of en or fr will return the appropriate results. To support pagination, the API will now accept a min and max number for number of rows to start at or end at. By default, the data is returned for the first 10 rows, if you would like to request the next ten results, set min to 11 and max to 21. You must provide a number for both min and max to be provided accurate results.Theme filtering is now available based on the standard theme list of the CGP. You can pass one or many values to the API by separating the theme code with a comma. E.g. ‚Äúadministration, legal, society‚Äù. In this version, the total count for the number of rows is available in the return as ‚Äútotal‚Äù. This was created to enable pagination.Organisation filtering is now available based on the following value list. You can pass one or many values to the API by separating the values with a ‚Äú|‚Äù. E.g. - ‚ÄúCanadian Space Agency|National Defence‚Äù. Type filtering is now available based on the following value list. You can pass one or many values to the API by separating the values with a ‚Äú|‚Äù. E.g. - ‚ÄúDataset|Collection‚Äù. Foundational filtering is now available. By passing ‚Äútrue‚Äù to the API only results for the query that have been tagged as a foundational layer will be returned. / L'API prendra le param√®tre du mot-cl√© et interrogera les champs de m√©tadonn√©es applicables √† la recherche par mot-cl√©. Si la recherche g√©ospatiale est s√©lectionn√©e, les r√©sultats sont ensuite soumis √† une requ√™te d'intersection g√©ospatiale bas√©e sur le rectangle de d√©limitation cr√©√© √† partir des param√®tres nord, est, sud et ouest. Les r√©sultats renvoy√©s sont tous les enregistrements de m√©tadonn√©es contenant le mot-cl√© qui se croisent avec le rectangle de d√©limitation. Le r√©sultat est un tableau d'objets JSON. L'API est bilingue, et le fait de passer le param√®tre de langue en ou fr renverra les r√©sultats appropri√©s. Pour prendre en charge la pagination, l'API accepte d√©sormais un nombre minimal et maximal de lignes pour le nombre de lignes de d√©part ou de fin. Par d√©faut, les donn√©es sont renvoy√©es pour les 10 premi√®res lignes, si vous souhaitez demander les dix r√©sultats suivants, d√©finissez min √† 11 et max √† 21. Vous devez fournir un nombre √† la fois pour min et max pour obtenir des r√©sultats pr√©cis.Le filtrage par th√®me est maintenant disponible sur la base de la liste de th√®mes standard du CGP. Vous pouvez transmettre une ou plusieurs valeurs √† l'API en s√©parant le code du th√®me par une virgule. Par exemple, &quot;administration, juridique, soci√©t√©&quot;. Dans cette version, le compte total pour le nombre de lignes est disponible dans le retour comme &quot;total&quot;. Le filtrage des organisations est maintenant disponible sur la base de la liste de valeurs suivante. Vous pouvez passer une ou plusieurs valeurs √† l'API en s√©parant les valeurs par un &quot;|&quot;. Par exemple : &quot;Agence spatiale canadienne|D√©fense nationale&quot;. Le filtrage par type est d√©sormais disponible sur la base de la liste de valeurs suivante. Vous pouvez transmettre une ou plusieurs valeurs √† l'API en les s√©parant par un &quot;|&quot;. Par exemple : &quot;Dataset|Collection&quot;. Le filtrage fondamental est d√©sormais disponible. En passant &quot;true&quot; √† l'API, seuls les r√©sultats de la requ√™te qui ont √©t√© √©tiquet√©s comme couche de base seront renvoy√©s.</div>





    <h3 class="field-label">Query parameters</h3>
    <div class="field-items">
      <div class="param">keyword_only (optional)</div>
      
            <div class="param-desc"><span class="param-type">Query Parameter</span> &mdash; For keyword only searches, pass the value of true or false / Pour les recherches par mot-cl√© uniquement, passez la valeur true ou false. </div>      <div class="param">keyword (optional)</div>
      
            <div class="param-desc"><span class="param-type">Query Parameter</span> &mdash; Keyword used for querying / Mot cl√© utilis√© pour l&#x27;interrogation </div>      <div class="param">lang (optional)</div>
      
            <div class="param-desc"><span class="param-type">Query Parameter</span> &mdash; Language of result / Langue du r√©sultat </div>      <div class="param">min (optional)</div>
      
            <div class="param-desc"><span class="param-type">Query Parameter</span> &mdash; Minimum row number for returned results / Nombre minimal de lignes pour les r√©sultats retourn√©s </div>      <div class="param">max (optional)</div>
      
            <div class="param-desc"><span class="param-type">Query Parameter</span> &mdash; Maximum row number for returned results / Nombre maximal de lignes pour les r√©sultats retourn√©s </div>      <div class="param">theme (optional)</div>
      
            <div class="param-desc"><span class="param-type">Query Parameter</span> &mdash; Theme filtering is based on the standard theme list of the CGP.     <h3 class="field-label">Produces</h3>
    This API call produces the following media types according to the <span class="header">Accept</span> request header;
    the media type will be conveyed by the <span class="header">Content-Type</span> response header.
    <ul>
      <li><code>application/json</code></li>
    </ul>

    Query Results / R√©sultats des requ√™tes

    <a class="up" href="#__Methods">Up</a>
    <pre class="get"><code class="huge"><span class="http-method">get</span> /id</code></pre></div>

  <h1><a name="TranslateTraduire">Translate / Traduire</a></h1>
  <div class="method"><a name="translate"></a>
    <div class="method-path">
    <a class="up" href="#__Methods">Up</a>
    <pre class="get"><code class="huge"><span class="http-method">get</span> /translate</code></pre></div>
    <div class="method-summary">translate text to given language / traduire un texte dans une langue donn√©e (<span class="nickname">translate</span>)</div>
    <div class="method-notes">translate text to given language / traduire un texte dans une langue donn√©e</div>





    <h3 class="field-label">Query parameters</h3>
    <div class="field-items">
      <div class="param">text (optional)</div>
      
            <div class="param-desc"><span class="param-type">Query Parameter</span> &mdash; text to be translated / texte √† traduire </div>      <div class="param">from_lang (optional)</div>
      
            <div class="param-desc"><span class="param-type">Query Parameter</span> &mdash; from text language / du langage textuel </div>      <div class="param">to_lang (optional)</div>
      
            <div class="param-desc"><span class="param-type">Query Parameter</span> &mdash; to text language / au langage textuel </div>    </div>  <!-- field-items -->


    <h3 class="field-label">Return type</h3>
    <div class="return-type">
      <a href="#translate">translate</a>
      
    </div>

    <!--Todo: process Response Object and its headers, schema, examples -->

    <h3 class="field-label">Example data</h3>
    <div class="example-data-content-type">Content-Type: application/json</div>
    <pre class="example"><code>{
  "from_lang" : "from_lang",
  "to_lang" : "to_lang",
  "text" : "text"
}</code></pre>

    <h3 class="field-label">Produces</h3>
    This API call produces the following media types according to the <span class="header">Accept</span> request header;
    the media type will be conveyed by the <span class="header">Content-Type</span> response header.
    <ul>
      <li><code>application/json</code></li>
    </ul>

    <h3 class="field-label">Responses</h3>
    <h4 class="field-label">200</h4>
    translate text to given language / traduire un texte dans une langue donn√©e
        <a href="#translate">translate</a>
    <h4 class="field-label">400</h4>
    bad input parameters
        <a href="#"></a>
  </div> <!-- method -->
